    set net.ipv4.ip_forward 1
    set net.ipv4.tcp_fin_timeout 30

    bind Guest
    enable
!

interface WifiMaster0
compatibility BGN+AX
tx-burst
beamforming explicit
downlink-mumimo
uplink-mumimo
spatial-reuse
up
!
interface WifiMaster0/AccessPoint0
rename AccessPoint
description &quot;Wi-Fi access point&quot;
security-level private
wps
wmm
rrm
ft mdid auto
ft enable
up
!
interface WifiMaster0/AccessPoint1
rename GuestWiFi
description &quot;Guest access point&quot;
ssid Guest
wmm
rrm
ft mdid auto
ft enable
down
!
interface Bridge0
include WifiMaster0/AccessPoint0
!
interface GigabitEthernet0/Vlan3
description &quot;Guest VLAN&quot;
security-level protected
up
!
interface Bridge1
rename Guest
description &quot;Guest network&quot;
inherit GigabitEthernet0/Vlan3
include WifiMaster0/AccessPoint1
security-level protected
ip address 10.1.30.1 255.255.255.0
peer-isolation
!
!
interface WifiMaster1
compatibility AN+AC+AX
tx-burst
beamforming explicit
downlink-mumimo
uplink-mumimo
spatial-reuse
up
!
interface WifiMaster1/AccessPoint0
rename AccessPoint_5G
description &quot;5GHz Wi-Fi access point&quot;
security-level private
wps
wmm
follow WifiMaster0/AccessPoint0
up
!
interface WifiMaster1/AccessPoint1
rename GuestWiFi_5G
description &quot;5GHz Guest access point&quot;
follow WifiMaster0/AccessPoint1
down
!
interface Bridge0
include WifiMaster1/AccessPoint0
iapp auto
!
interface Guest
include WifiMaster1/AccessPoint1
iapp auto
!
!
ip dhcp pool _WEBADMIN_GUEST_AP
range 10.1.30.33 120
bind Guest
!
ip nat Guest
!
interface ISP
ip dhcp client displace Guest
!
!
